Алгоритм кратко:

Строим минимальное остовное дерево с нуля.

1. Сортируем рёбра исходного графа по неубыванию их весов
2. Добавляем ребро в остовное дерево если одна его вершина уже находится в остовном дереве, а другая нет
3. Алгоритм завершается, когда в основном дереве присутствуют все вершины ^Zb1QVRxu

Рёбра в отсортированном порядке:

Алгоритм Прима ^tjtXmQiq

Алгоритм кратко:

Строим остовное дерево с нуля.

Стартовой точкой выбираем любую вершину

1. Рассматриваем соседей вершины
2. Выбираем соседа, до которого идёт ребро с минимальным весом
3. Добавляем этого соседа в остовное дерево
4. Рассматриваем его соседей + оставшиеся с предыдущего шага рёбра ^O9V2Fno9

Код на Python:


import heapq


class UnionSet:
    def __init__(self, n):
        self.parent = [i for i in range(n)]
        self.rank = [1 for _ in range(n)]

    def find(self, x):
        if x == self.parent[x]:
            return x
        else:
            self.parent[x] = self.find(self.parent[x])
            return self.parent[x]

    def union(self, x, y):
        x_root = self.find(x)
        y_root = self.find(y)
        if x_root == y_root:
            return
        if self.rank[x_root] > self.rank[y_root]:
            self.parent[y_root] = x_root
        elif self.rank[x_root] < self.rank[y_root]:
            self.parent[x_root] = y_root
        else:
            self.parent[y_root] = x_root
            self.rank[x_root] += 1

    def is_same(self, x, y):
        return self.find(x) == self.find(y)


def kruskal(graph):
    edges = list()
    for v in range(len(graph)):
        for u, w in enumerate(graph[v]):
            if w != 0:
                edges.append((w, v, u))
    edges.sort()

    min_spanning_tree = list()
    num_taken = 0

    union_set = UnionSet(len(graph))

    for i in range(len(edges)):
        if num_taken == len(graph) - 1:
            break
        w, u, v = edges[i]
        if not union_set.is_same(u, v):
            num_taken += 1
            min_spanning_tree.append(edges[i])
            union_set.union(u, v)

    return min_spanning_tree
 ^uOvD1XXQ

Код на Python:


import heapq


def add_edges(graph, v, taken, edges):
    taken[v] = True
    for i, w in enumerate(graph[v]):
        if w != 0 and not taken[i]:
            heapq.heappush(edges, (w, i, v))


def prim(graph):
    taken = [False] * len(graph)
    edges = list()
    add_edges(graph, 0, taken, edges)

    min_spanning_tree = list()
    num_taken = 0
    while len(edges) > 0 and num_taken < len(graph) - 1:
        w, v, u = heapq.heappop(edges)
        if not taken[v]:
            num_taken += 1
            min_spanning_tree.append((u, v, w))
            add_edges(graph, v, taken, edges)

    return min_spanning_tree
 ^gQE51wwm

Код на C++:


#include <queue>
#include <tuple>
#include <vector>

typedef std::tuple<int, int, int> Edge;

void add_edges(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph,
               int v, std::vector<bool> &taken,
               std::priority_queue<Edge> &edges) {
    taken[v] = true;
    for (int i = 0; i < graph[v].size(); ++i) {
        int w = graph[v][i];
        if (w != 0 and not taken[i]) {
            edges.push(Edge(w, i, v));
        }
    }
}

std::vector<Edge> prim(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph) {
    std::vector<bool> taken(graph.size(), false);
    std::priority_queue<Edge> edges;
    add_edges(graph, 0, taken, edges);

    std::vector<Edge> min_spanning_tree;
    int num_taken = 0;

    while (not edges.empty() and num_taken < graph.size() - 1) {
        Edge edge = edges.top();
        edges.pop();
        int w, v, u;
        std::tie(w, v, u) = edge;
        if (not taken[v]) {
            ++num_taken;
            min_spanning_tree.push_back(edge);
            add_edges(graph, v, taken, edges);
        }
    }

    return min_spanning_tree;
}
 ^zArpTMBo

Код на C++:


#include <algorithm>
#include <tuple>
#include <vector>

struct UnionSet {
    UnionSet(int n) {
        for (int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
            parent.push_back(i);
            rank.push_back(0);
        }
    }

    int find(int x) {
        if (parent[x] != x) {
            parent[x] = find(parent[x]);
        }
        return parent[x];
    }

    void unite(int x, int y) {
        int x_root = find(x);
        int y_root = find(y);
        if (x_root == y_root) {
            return;
        }
        if (rank[x_root] < rank[y_root]) {
            parent[x_root] = y_root;
        } else if (rank[x_root] > rank[y_root]) {
            parent[y_root] = x_root;
        } else {
            parent[y_root] = x_root;
            rank[x_root]++;
        }
    }

    bool is_same(int x, int y) {
        return find(x) == find(y);
    }

    std::vector<int> parent;
    std::vector<int> rank;
};

typedef std::tuple<int, int, int> Edge;

std::vector<Edge> kruskal(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph) {
    std::vector<Edge> edges;
    for (int v = 0; v < graph.size(); v++) {
        for (int u = 0; u < graph[v].size(); u++) {
            if (graph[v][u] != 0)
                edges.push_back(std::make_tuple(graph[v][u], v, u));
        }
    }
    std::sort(edges.begin(), edges.end(), [](const Edge &a, const Edge &b) {
        return std::get<0>(a) < std::get<0>(b);
    });

    std::vector<Edge> min_spanning_tree;
    int num_taken = 0;

    UnionSet union_set(graph.size());

    for (int i = 0; i < edges.size(); i++) {
        if (num_taken == graph.size() - 1)
            break;
        Edge edge = edges[i];
        int weight = std::get<0>(edge);
        int v = std::get<1>(edge);
        int u = std::get<2>(edge);
        if (!union_set.is_same(v, u)) {
            union_set.unite(v, u);
            min_spanning_tree.push_back(edge);
            num_taken++;
            if (num_taken == graph.size() - 1) {
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    return min_spanning_tree;
}
 ^BpdIgEC6

			"text": "Код на C++:\n\n\n#include <queue>\n#include <tuple>\n#include <vector>\n\ntypedef std::tuple<int, int, int> Edge;\n\nvoid add_edges(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph,\n               int v, std::vector<bool> &taken,\n               std::priority_queue<Edge> &edges) {\n    taken[v] = true;\n    for (int i = 0; i < graph[v].size(); ++i) {\n        int w = graph[v][i];\n        if (w != 0 and not taken[i]) {\n            edges.push(Edge(w, i, v));\n        }\n    }\n}\n\nstd::vector<Edge> prim(const std::vector<std::vector<int>> &graph) {\n    std::vector<bool> taken(graph.size(), false);\n    std::priority_queue<Edge> edges;\n    add_edges(graph, 0, taken, edges);\n\n    std::vector<Edge> min_spanning_tree;\n    int num_taken = 0;\n\n    while (not edges.empty() and num_taken < graph.size() - 1) {\n        Edge edge = edges.top();\n        edges.pop();\n        int w, v, u;\n        std::tie(w, v, u) = edge;\n        if (not taken[v]) {\n            ++num_taken;\n            min_spanning_tree.push_back(edge);\n            add_edges(graph, v, taken, edges);\n        }\n    }\n\n    return min_spanning_tree;\n}\n",

v < graph.size(); v++) {\n        for (int u = 0; u < graph[v].size(); u++) {\n            if (graph[v][u] != 0)\n                edges.push_back(std::make_tuple(graph[v][u], v, u));\n        }\n    }\n    std::sort(edges.begin(), edges.end(), [[const Edge &a, const Edge &b]] {\n        return std::get<0>(a) < std::get<0>(b);\n    });\n\n    std::vector<Edge> min_spanning_tree;\n    int num_taken = 0;\n\n    UnionSet union_set(graph.size());\n\n    for (int i = 0; i < edges.size(); i++) {\n        if (num_taken == graph.size() - 1)\n            break;\n        Edge edge = edges[i];\n        int weight = std::get<0>(edge);\n        int v = std::get<1>(edge);\n        int u = std::get<2>(edge);\n        if (!union_set.is_same(v, u)) {\n            union_set.unite(v, u);\n            min_spanning_tree.push_back(edge);\n            num_taken++;\n            if (num_taken == graph.size() - 1) {\n                break;\n            }\n        }\n    }\n\n    return min_spanning_tree;\n}\n",
